var prevScrollpos = window.pageYOffset;

    document.getElementById("masthead").style.top = "0";

}

<h3 style="font-size:1.33em; margin-top:0;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0;margin-right:0;" class="has-text-align-left has-link-color wp-elements-214890facf0eb063878f5ab128c9cfe6 wp-block-post-title has-text-color has-ast-global-color-0-color"><a href="https://momathomeonline.com/parenting/parenting-basics/parenting-styles-are-you-following-the-right-one-for-your-child/" target="_self" >Parenting Styles: Are You Following the Right One for Your Child?</a></h3>

<div class="taxonomy-category has-text-align-left wp-block-post-terms"><a href="https://momathomeonline.com/category/parenting/parenting-basics/" rel="tag">Parenting Basics</a></div>


<div class="wp-block-group is-content-justification-left is-layout-flex wp-container-core-group-is-layout-79128019 wp-block-group-is-layout-flex"><div class="has-text-align-center wp-block-post-author"><div class="wp-block-post-author__content"><p class="wp-block-post-author__name"><a href="https://momathomeonline.com/author/maho/" target="_self">Shiboli Jana</a></p></div></div>


<p class="has-text-align-center has-ast-global-color-1-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-5bdd8f2ea741e0ff862dcf41a05e822e" style="margin-top:0;margin-right:0;margin-bottom:0;margin-left:0"> • </p>


<div class="has-text-align-center has-link-color wp-elements-a7806fa60124d4e42efaa3e74be2e290 wp-block-post-date has-text-color has-ast-global-color-1-color"><time datetime="2023-08-23T13:34:04+05:30">August 23, 2023</time></div>

</div>


<div class="wp-block-post-excerpt"><p class="wp-block-post-excerpt__excerpt">Study how parenting styles &#8211; authoritarian, authoritative, permissive, and uninvolved &#8211; shape diverse child development. Tailor your approach with flexibility, empathy, and self-awareness for optimal results.</p><p class="wp-block-post-excerpt__more-text"><a class="wp-block-post-excerpt__more-link" href="https://momathomeonline.com/parenting/parenting-basics/parenting-styles-are-you-following-the-right-one-for-your-child/">Read More&#8230; </a></p></div></div>

</li><li data-wp-key="post-template-item-115" class="wp-block-post post-115 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-parenting-tips ast-article-single">

( ( [ dropdownId, homeUrl ] ) => {
		const dropdown = document.getElementById( dropdownId );
		function onSelectChange() {
			setTimeout( () => {
				if ( 'escape' === dropdown.dataset.lastkey ) {
					return;
				}
				if ( dropdown.value ) {
					location.href = dropdown.value;
				}
			}, 250 );
		}
		function onKeyUp( event ) {
			if ( 'Escape' === event.key ) {
				dropdown.dataset.lastkey = 'escape';
			} else {
				delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
			}
		}
		function onClick() {
			delete dropdown.dataset.lastkey;
		}
		dropdown.addEventListener( 'keyup', onKeyUp );
		dropdown.addEventListener( 'click', onClick );
		dropdown.addEventListener( 'change', onSelectChange );
	} )( ["wp-block-archives-2","https://momathomeonline.com"] );
